    <component is="script" >        $(function() {
            $('.daterange').daterangepicker({
                'linkedCalendars': false,
                'showCustomRangeLabel': false,
                                                'opens': 'center',
                'drops': 'auto',
                'locale': { 'cancelLabel': 'Clear' },
            }, function (start, end, label) {
                let container = $('#game-logs');
                $('input[name="from"]', container).val(start.format('YYYY-MM-DD'));
                $('input[name="to"]', container).val(end.format('YYYY-MM-DD'));
                changeGameLogsFilter();
            }).on('cancel.daterangepicker', function(ev, picker) {
                let container = $('#game-logs');
                $('input[name="from"]', container).val('');
                $('input[name="to"]', container).val('');
                changeGameLogsFilter();
            });

            $('.daterange-opener').click(function() {
                $('.daterange').click();
            });
        });
    </component>                    </div>

                            <div class="SectionTitle"> Player Biography and Trivia </div>
                            <div class="pera">
                                
                                
                                
                                                                                                            <p> Cult/Star player for <a href="https://www.eliteprospects.com/team/186/avangard-omsk"> Avangard Omsk </a> </p>
                                                                            <p> Cult/Star player for <a href="https://www.eliteprospects.com/team/1095/heki"> HeKi </a> </p>
                                                                            <p> Cult/Star player for <a href="https://www.eliteprospects.com/team/44/pelicans"> Pelicans </a> </p>
                                                                    
                                                                    <p><b>Career Transactions</b><br>
- 2012-01-12 • Rights traded to the Calgary Flames w/ <a href="player.php?player=9104">Mike Cammalleri</a> & a 2012 5th round pick (<a href="player.php?player=88706">Ryan Culkin</a>) for <a href="player.php?player=9089">Rene Bourque</a>, the rights to <a href="player.php?player=26390">Patrick Holland</a> & a 2013 2nd round pick (<a href="player.php?player=126396">Zach Fucale</a>)<br>
- 2010-08-16 • Rights traded to the Montreal Canadiens by Tampa Bay for <a href="player.php?player=11518">Cédrick Desjardins</a><br>
- 2009-06-23 • Signed by Avangard Omsk to a 2 year contract<br>
</p>
